      </td>\n        <td>\n         300\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">\n        Transportation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Transportation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bus">\n        Bus\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Bus">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The Annapolis Department of Transportation (ADOT) provides bus service with eight routes, collectively branded\n       <a href="/wiki/Annapolis_Transit" title="Annapolis Transit">\n        Annapolis Transit\n       </a>\n       . The system serves the city with recreational areas, shopping centers, educational and medical facilities, and employment hubs. ADOT also offers transportation for the elderly and persons with disabilities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland_Transit_Administration" title="Maryland Transit Administration">\n        Maryland Transit Administration\n       </a>\n       commuter buses also allow for access to Baltimore or Washington, D.C.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government">\n        Government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="City_government">\n        City government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: City government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2112" data-file-width="2816" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG/220px-Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG/330px-Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG/440px-Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Annapolis_City_Hall_2.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Annapolis City Hall\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Annapolis is governed via the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weak_mayor" title="Weak mayor">\n        weak mayor\n       </a>\n       system. The city council consists of eight aldermen who are elected from single member wards. The mayor is elected directly in a citywide vote. Since 2008, several aldermen have introduced unsuccessful charter amendments to institute a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Council-manager" title="Council-manager">\n        council-manager\n       </a>\n       system, a move opposed by both Democratic mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Joshua_J._Cohen" title="Joshua J. Cohen">\n        Joshua J. Cohen\n       </a>\n       and his Republican successor\n       <a href="/wiki/Mike_Pantelides" title="Mike Pantelides">\n        Mike Pantelides\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="State_government">\n        State government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: State government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland_General_Assembly" title="Maryland General Assembly">\n        state legislature\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Maryland" title="Governor of Maryland">\n        governor\'s office\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland_Court_of_Appeals" title="Maryland Court of Appeals">\n        appellate courts\n       </a>\n       are located in Annapolis. While Annapolis is the state\'s only\n       <a href="/wiki/Capital_city" title="Capital city">\n        capital\n       </a>\n       , some administrative offices, including a number of\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Cabinet-level_departments&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cabinet-level departments (page does not exist)">\n        cabinet-level departments\n       </a>\n       , are based in\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">\n        Baltimore\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">\n        Education\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Education">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Annapolis is served by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Anne_Arundel_County_Public_Schools" title="Anne Arundel County Public Schools">\n        Anne Arundel County Public Schools\n       </a>\n       system.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Founded in 1896,\n       <a href="/wiki/Annapolis_High_School_(Maryland)" title="Annapolis High School (Maryland)">\n        Annapolis High School\n       </a>\n       has an internationally recognized\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Baccalaureate" title="International Baccalaureate">\n        IB International Program\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/St._Mary%27s_High_School_(Annapolis,_Maryland)" title="St. Mary\'s High School (Annapolis, Maryland)">\n        St. Mary\'s High School\n       </a>\n       and Elementary School are located in downtown Annapolis on Spa Creek. St. Anne\'s School of Annapolis,\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Eastport_Elementary_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Eastport Elementary School (page does not exist)">\n        Eastport Elementary School\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Aleph_Bet_Jewish_Day_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Aleph Bet Jewish Day School (page does not exist)">\n        Aleph Bet Jewish Day School\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Annapolis_Area_Christian_School" title="Annapolis Area Christian School">\n        Annapolis Area Christian School\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=St._Martins_Lutheran_School&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="St. Martins Lutheran School (page does not exist)">\n        St. Martins Lutheran School\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Severn_School" title="Severn School">\n        Severn School\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Indian_Creek_School" title="Indian Creek School">\n        Indian Creek School\n       </a>\n       are also in the Annapolis area. The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Key_School" title="Key School">\n        Key School\n       </a>\n       , located on a converted farm in the neighborhood of Hillsmere, has also served Annapolis for over 50 years. Anne Arundel County\'s alternative high school,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mary_E._Moss_Academy" title="Mary E. Moss Academy">\n        Mary E. Moss Academy\n       </a>\n       , is also in the Annapolis area.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Public High Schools that serve students in the Annapolis area:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Annapolis_High_School_(Maryland)" title="Annapolis High School (Maryland)">\n         Annapolis High School\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a High School">\n         Broadneck High School\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Old_Mill_High_School" title="Old Mill High School">\n         Old Mill High School\n   <a href="/wiki/Southern_High_School_(Harwood)" title="Southern High School (Harwood)">\n         Southern High School\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a    </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="282" data-file-width="350" height="177" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/40/Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png/220px-Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/40/Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png/330px-Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/4/40/Chesapeake_Bayhawks_logo.png 2x"  </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bayhawks" title="Chesapeake Bayhawks">\n          Chesapeake Bayhawks\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On March 9, 2010, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bayhawks" title="Chesapeake Bayhawks">\n        Chesapeake Bayhawks\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Lacrosse" title="Major League Lacrosse">\n        Major League Lacrosse\n       </a>\n       moved from Washington D.C. to the Annapolis area, at\n       <a href="/wiki/Navy%E2%80%93Marine_Corps_Memorial_Stadium" title="Navy\xe2\x80\x93Marine Corps Memorial Stadium">\n        Navy\xe2\x80\x93Marine Corps Memorial Stadium\n       </a>\n       . In\n       <a href="/wiki/2013_Major_League_Lacrosse_season" title="2013 Major League Lacrosse season">\n        2013\n       </a>\n       , the Bayhawks won the league\'s championship, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Steinfeld_Cup" title="Steinfeld Cup">\n        Steinfeld Cup\n       </a>\n       , for the fifth time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n        <a href="#cite_note-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Parks_and_recreation">\n        Parks and recreation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annapolis,_Maryland&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Parks and recreation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       The City boasts over 200 acres (81\xc2\xa0ha) of parkland,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with the largest park being the 70-acre\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Truxtun_Heights_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Truxtun Heights Park (page does not exist)">\n        Truxtun Heights Park\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The city is also home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Quiet_Waters_Park_(Maryland)" title="Quiet Waters Park (Maryland)">\n        Quiet Waters Park\n       </a>\n       , a 340-acre park run by Anne Arundel County.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n  </a>\n       </i>\n       covers the news of Annapolis and Anne Arundel County See also:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_newspapers_in_Maryland_in_the_18th-century" title="List of
